Telegram from Jinan (Title Omitted): The situation of the breach of the Juancheng River has been reported to the Central Government in previous telegrams. The severity of this Yellow River flood is unprecedented. The water in the Shaanxi and Luoyang areas rose sharply, and the water from the upper reaches came down in layers, waves, and raging roars, pouring into Shandong Province. Although soldiers, workers, and civilians desperately tried to protect it, human power could not turn the tide, and the Li Sheng Tun 民埝 in Juancheng County and the levee between Dongzhuang and Linpuji were overflowed and collapsed, with a total of six breaches, more than 200 zhang wide. The overflowing water was divided into two streams, passing through the Yincheng 引馬集 Juancheng Huang'an area, one heading towards Heze 北　, and turning northeast at the Qili River, rejoining into one, rushing straight and flooding without returning. Coupled with continuous heavy rain, the water situation is becoming more and more serious. The Jiangsu Dam has now been completely submerged. Although various places have built surfaces to control the water, the water is too fierce and fails step by step. Wherever the water reaches, Juancheng 鄣城 Heze 鉅野 are the most severely affected, with water everywhere. Other counties such as Wenshang, Jiaxiang, Jining, Dongping, Yanggu, and Shouzhang also have extremely heavy disasters. I have now received a telegram from Chairman Li Yizhi on the 13th, stating that 60-70% of the water has flowed out of the mouth, and the entire river is pouring down, which is extremely critical. According to a report from Regional Inspector Wang Shaochang, the water between 鄲城鉅野 is more than 70 li wide. According to the current situation, the disaster area has grown to more than 200 li long and 70-80 li wide. Fields, gardens, houses, and graves have all become swamps. 　Grain　shoes have been given to the water gods. As for the situation of the people in the disaster area, those who have escaped to the堤 are eating in the wind and sleeping in the open, with no way to make a living. Those who are still trapped in the water are calling to the heavens and earth, and are waiting to die. The cries of sorrow are everywhere, and it is unbearable to hear. It is difficult to predict the extent of the disaster. The number of villages and the number of disaster-stricken people in the disaster area also need to be investigated. In short, this flood is several times more serious than the breach in Dongming the year before last. Since the people of more than a dozen counties in western Shandong suffered from the Dongming flood, their vitality has been depleted, and their wounds have not yet healed. This spring, the drought was rampant, and the two wheats failed. A few days ago, the rain had just been sufficient, and we were hoping for a good autumn harvest, but an extraordinary event occurred, and we were again in a predicament. Alas, my people, how can they bear this? As 榘, I have failed in my duty, and I cannot prevent it in advance, nor can I save it afterwards. I am guilty before the gods and ashamed before public opinion. I am bewildered at midnight and cannot sleep or eat. For the present plan, in addition to sending personnel with disaster relief funds to various counties for verification and distribution, it is not enough to save the dying people without providing extensive relief. Without quickly筹堵决, it is not enough to reverse the bad luck in the future. However, the disaster is so serious, and the project is so huge. It is difficult to consider both. In this time of extreme scarcity of funds, even if we dig and scrape everything, it will be a drop in the bucket, and it will not help. After thinking again and again, I have to cry out loudly and ask for life for the people. I only hope that Hong Bao will量与之,推 Hunger drowning with the怀, 特沛恩施,优予倾助, to 淡沈 the disaster and卹 the people's lives. Shandong is very fortunate, the overall situation is very fortunate. Exhausted, I beg for your consideration. Shandong Provincial Government Chairman Han Fuqu叩删 (15th) You secret,

Current Commentary

Epidemic Prevention Movement 57

— Year

For a week, the temperature has increased quite sharply. According to the report from the Xujiahui Observatory, the highest temperature in Shanghai was only 91 degrees on the 9th. On the 10th, it suddenly rose to 95.5 degrees. On the 13th, at the beginning of the hottest period, it reached 97 degrees. On the 14th, it exceeded 100 degrees. In the past two days, it has also been around 100 degrees. Related news appearing in this newspaper includes a sharp increase in the number of patients with seasonal diseases in various hospitals and the intensified implementation of the epidemic prevention movement in this city. The meaning of "prevention" is to think of potential problems and prepare for them in advance. Now, while seasonal diseases have not yet become a serious problem, taking early measures to prevent them is indeed a wise move by the health authorities of this city and should be emulated nationwide.

Among the nine legally defined infectious diseases in our country, cholera is most commonly discovered during the hottest period and is extremely virulent. Therefore, it is acceptable to say that the focus of summer epidemic prevention work is preventing the occurrence of cholera. This disease was rampant throughout China in 1932. According to statistics from over 300 cities surveyed, there were 100,000 patients, and the death toll exceeded 30,000. In that year, Shanghai, due to its residents' living conditions being conducive to the spread of the disease, had over 4,000 infected people citywide. However, only 317 people died, with a mortality rate of only 7.4% (detailed in the 1934 Shen Bao Yearbook). This indicates that Shanghai's efforts in epidemic prevention were more intensive than those of other cities. In the past two years, very few cases of this disease have been discovered, partly due to the effectiveness of large-scale preventive vaccinations and partly due to the disease's tendency to have a major outbreak every three or four years (detailed in Table 15 of Dr. Gao Jinglang's book on infectious diseases in children).

The easiest way to start epidemic prevention work is to popularize preventive vaccinations. According to Mr. Jin Baoshan of the Health Facilities Experimental Center, who compiled the "1934 Epidemic Prevention Facilities Situation" for this newspaper's yearbook, over 749,000 people in Shanghai had received preventive vaccinations by the end of August. Although this may not be the sole reason for the low incidence of epidemic diseases this year, its effectiveness can be generally seen. This year, as previously reported in this newspaper, only 265,000 people in Shanghai have been vaccinated, only one-third of last year's number. This is a fact that the Shanghai health authorities should pay attention to in the epidemic prevention movement. Furthermore, the 3.5 million people living in areas prone to epidemic diseases should not be negligent and complacent simply because there have been no epidemics for two years. As for those in charge of epidemic prevention in other regions, we especially hope that they will pay attention to popularizing preventive vaccinations.

The means of transmitting infectious diseases include unclean drinking water, food, flies, and carriers. Of these, drinking water requires the most attention. Regarding the other factors, anyone with basic hygiene knowledge can often prevent transmission through personal efforts. However, even in places like London and Hamburg, where public health services are well-developed, unclean drinking water can still cause harm. In the Suzhou Creek in Shanghai, bacteriophages that resist cholera were discovered during the major epidemic of 1932. We hope that the local health authorities will conduct research on this. In inland areas, people lack hygiene knowledge, and polluted waterways cause significant harm. Local administrative and self-governance personnel must carry out disinfection work as soon as possible. Shanghai undertook this work in 1934. How effective it was and what lessons were learned should be publicized to serve as a model for the entire country.

This reporter has not personally witnessed epidemic prevention efforts, so my comments may be criticized as unwarranted concern. However, being prepared leads to success, while being unprepared leads to failure. If we only start discussing disaster prevention after seeing the water level rise, we will expend more effort and achieve less. The lessons of the past are not far off. The people of our country should take them to heart.

Italian Troops Mobilizing for Ethiopia Reach 180,000; Mussolini May Fly to Give Speech; Denies Making New Demands on Abyssinia 58

(Rome) Today, the Propaganda Department issued a communique announcing new measures taken by Italy in its army and navy. It is generally believed that the purpose of this communique is to inform all countries that Italy's military preparations are proceeding openly and will not be affected by any foreign interference. According to the communique, two more army divisions were mobilized today, and all mobilization plans have been fully implemented. There are now over 1,000 military aircraft available for attack. A total of ten divisions have been mobilized, including five regular army infantry divisions, each with 13,000 men: (1) the "Gaverglia" Division, (2) the "Bellolida" Division, (3) the "Sapodda" Division, (4) the "Gransano" Division, and (5) the "Silah" Division. There are also five Party militia divisions, each with 10,000 men: (1) the "March 23rd" Division, (2) the "April 21st" Division, (3) the "October 28th" Division, (4) the "January 3rd" Division, and (5) the "February 1st" Division. These names represent the most important dates in the history of the Fascist Party. In addition, there are approximately 35,000 troops permanently stationed in Italian East Africa, including over 14,000 in Tripolitania and Cyrenaica, 3,500 in Eritrea, and 3,200 in Somalia. There are also 35,000 specialized workers and technicians who have been sent to East Africa to build and repair roads. Once the project is completed, Prime Minister Mussolini will personally inspect it. In total, Italy has 185,000 troops in East Africa, including specialized workers. (Havas dispatch, 15th)

(Rome) Today's government gazette states that Italy, in view of Abyssinia's urgent preparations for war, must also take further military action. After Mussolini ordered the mobilization of two new divisions yesterday, the Italian expeditionary force to Ethiopia will reach 160,000 men. In addition, there are many soldiers in Italian Somalia. Today, Mussolini also requisitioned automobile drivers from the classes of 1909, 1910, and 1912, as well as dispatched additional combat aircraft and personnel to Ethiopia. At the same time, he ordered munitions factories to accelerate production. Mussolini himself is anxiously coordinating everything day and night in the Palazzo Venezia. (National Telegram, 15th)

(Rome) It is expected that Mussolini will fly to Italian Eritrea in East Africa within the next few days to inspect the troops assembled there and deliver a speech encouraging the soldiers before the war against Ethiopia. Well-informed sources here deny that Italy has made any suggestions for resolving the dispute. The new military plan announced by the Italian Prime Minister yesterday was prominently featured on the front pages of all newspapers, with an even more determined attitude than before. The "Lavoro Fascista" newspaper stated that while European foreign ministries are endlessly discussing the legal interpretations of the so-called Abyssinian question and possible political adjustments, Prime Minister Mussolini is working hard. The Prime Minister, now the mastermind of political strategy, has stated that this is the only way to safeguard Italy's rights and glorify its future. (Reuters dispatch, 16th)

(Rome) This year's Italian army summer exercises are scheduled for the end of August. They are of great importance and scale. More than seven divisions of troops with full combat readiness will participate in the exercises in the Bolsano area. Three divisions each will participate in Milan and Naples, and four divisions will participate in exercises near Udine. (National Telegram, 16th)

(Rome) The government has decided to hold large-scale army exercises in Italy within days. In terms of the number of participants, the scale of these exercises is unprecedented. The entire force will be divided into five groups to perform separately: one group in the Bolsano area, with seven army divisions; one group in the Udine area, with four army divisions; one group in the Milan area, with three army divisions; and one group in the Naples and Bari areas, with three army divisions. All will participate in the large-scale exercises simultaneously. (Havas dispatch, 15th)

Italy's New Naval Strength 59

(Rome) The government has recently announced, in accordance with the decision of the Naval General Staff, that it will begin construction of ten new submarines, which are expected to be launched by the end of this year. It is generally believed that this decision is a direct response to the Anglo-German Naval Agreement and is intended to increase the safety of transporting troops and supplies to East Africa via the Suez Canal. As of September of last year, Italy's navy had a total tonnage of 370,589 tons. Its current strength is as follows:

(1) Six battleships (two of which, each of 35,000 tons, were started in June of last year and are not yet completed; the remaining four each weigh 22,000 tons)

(2) One aircraft carrier

(3) Thirty cruisers (six of which are currently in dry dock for repairs)

(4) One hundred and eleven destroyers (twelve of which have not yet been launched)

(5) Seventy-seven submarines (totaling 55,524 tons; the ten to be built this month are not included) (Havas dispatch, 15th)

The Current Status of Diplomatic Negotiations 60

(London) Foreign Secretary Hoare stated in the House of Commons today that if a reconciliation in the Italo-Ethiopian dispute is not reached by August 25, the League of Nations Council will convene a meeting on that day. From this, it can be seen that the League of Nations has apparently abandoned its decision to meet on July 25. (National Telegram, 15th)

(London) The House of Commons will begin discussing the Italo-Ethiopian dispute next Tuesday. Lord Davies, the London District representative of the League of Nations Union, has submitted a motion in the House of Lords requesting immediate action, based on the Pact of Paris and the League of Nations Covenant, to resolve the Italo-Ethiopian dispute. (Havas dispatch, 16th)

(London) Current diplomatic efforts to mediate the Italo-Ethiopian dispute are aimed at preventing the League of Nations Council from meeting on July 25. It has therefore been suggested that the Italo-Ethiopian Mediation Committee, based on the League of Nations resolution of May 25, select a new member before July 25. It is unanimously acknowledged that the Mediation Committee cannot be expected to achieve anything during this period, but it is believed that extending the committee's life will allow the League of Nations to pass through another month, providing ample time for continued negotiations. This is the only way to reconcile the Italo-Ethiopian dispute. (National Telegram, 15th)

(London) It is reported that Italian Prime Minister Mussolini has rejected the idea of convening a tripartite conference of Britain, France, and Italy, using the 1906 tripartite treaty to discuss the Ethiopian question, believing that it would not achieve a resolution. Britain proposed a new suggestion at the end of last week, proposing that the British and French ambassadors in Rome consult with representatives of the Italian government to study the Ethiopian issue in light of the 1906 treaty, especially to jointly discuss the legal viewpoints and substantive events on which Italy based its actions towards Ethiopia in Geneva. Regarding this, well-informed sources point out that Italy has several grievances against Ethiopia, which it has never raised with the League of Nations, most notably Ethiopia's persistence in the slave system and obstruction of normal commercial relations between Ethiopia and Italian territories. Therefore, it is not an exaggeration to say that Ethiopia has not fulfilled its obligations under the League of Nations Covenant. At present, Italy has not yet responded to Britain's new proposal. As far as is generally known, the goal of the negotiations currently being held between the countries concerned is not so much to seek a peaceful resolution to the dispute as it is to find a way to explain Italy's reasons for attacking Ethiopia, which is more in line with the truth. (Havas dispatch, 15th)

African Djibouti: Yesterday, people in this French territory celebrated Democracy Memorial Day with Italian sailors, expressing French sympathy for Italy's position on Ethiopia. (National Telegram, 15th)

(London) The Daily Mail reports today that the British government has asked Mussolini to detail his grievances against Ethiopia for consideration at the next meeting of the League of Nations Council. The newspaper also said that if Mussolini agrees, the British government may support the issue of Italian trusteeship over Ethiopia, and may even argue that placing Ethiopia under Italian rule would be beneficial to Ethiopia. However, the key seems to be whether Italy's rule over its African territories has been successful. (National Telegram, 16th)

(Rome) Opposition to the League of Nations mediating the Italo-Ethiopian dispute is growing, as can be seen in today's editorial in the Gazzetta del Popolo. The newspaper claims that since the failure of the Italo-Ethiopian arbitration committee, the League of Nations' mediation efforts have proven to be completely ineffective. Therefore, the best solution is to officially end this effort. Allowing Ethiopia to be a member of the League of Nations was a major mistake that should be corrected. It should no longer be regarded as a member of the League of Nations, allowing it to test the League's credibility. This would be too much of a distortion of the facts, which Italy cannot tolerate. The article concludes that Italy is not only a large and visible member of the League of Nations, but also essential to maintaining the League's life. (National Telegram, 16th)

Ethiopia Has Been Preparing for War for Seven Months 61

(New York) According to Prince Tafari Makonnen, the cousin of the Ethiopian Emperor, who is studying here, the Ethiopian Emperor has been preparing for war for seven months. To defend against Italian attacks, munitions are stored in mountain caves, and underground tunnels have been built in the mountains to protect against aerial attacks. (Reuters dispatch, 15th)

Many Sympathize with Ethiopia 62

Fort Dodge, USA: Davis, a black man who served as a junior officer in Europe, is recruiting soldiers today to serve Ethiopia in the event of war with Italy. Authorities warned Davis that this recruitment violates international law, but he is still proceeding, asking recruits to travel to Ethiopia for public works projects. Davis has telegraphed the Ethiopian Emperor, stating that he intends to train an army of thousands. (National Telegram, 15th)

Miami, USA: The Black Fire has organized the Abyssinian Association to promote peace between Italy and Ethiopia. However, if peace fails, the association will train volunteers to serve in hospitals and ambulance services in Africa. (National Telegram, 15th)

(New York) People sympathetic to Ethiopia here have recently formed the Committee on the Ethiopian Question, chaired by Mr. Wickersham, the chairman of the Foreign Policy Association and a renowned expert on international law, along with prominent figures from various churches. The committee plans to petition President Roosevelt, asking the U.S. government to notify Italy that if it goes to war with Ethiopia, it will not be supported by American public opinion. The U.S. is prepared to mediate the Italo-Ethiopian dispute in the spirit of international justice. The committee has printed 500,000 copies of this petition for wide distribution, hoping that the result will be one million signatures. (Havas dispatch, 15th)

(Berlin) It was learned today that exiled Austrian National Socialists are mobilizing to assist Ethiopia in its war against Italy. (National Telegram, 15th)

Another Anti-Semitic Movement Erupts in Germany 63

(Berlin) Today, a film that excludes Jews was shown at the Western Cinema. Jewish viewers hissed and left their seats, causing a riot. A police patrol rushed to suppress it. Many evening newspapers criticized the Jews, with one newspaper saying that such actions were incomprehensible in the third year of the National Socialist government. (Reuters dispatch, 15th)

(Berlin) Another widespread nationwide anti-Semitic movement has recently erupted in Germany. It started last night when several National Socialist stormtroopers clashed with Jews on the street. Suddenly, the usually opulent Kurfürstendamm became chaotic, as the National Socialists considered the street to be the center of Jewish life. At that time, National Socialists smashed the windows of Jewish-owned shops. Although the police intervened, they were unable to stop the stormtroopers' actions. At the same time, anti-Semitic incidents were occurring in other cities. In Pleitenberg, Westphalia, a butcher named Lehoff requested that municipal authorities ban anti-Semitic movements. The National Socialists were furious and immediately launched a large-scale demonstration against him. In Rastenberg, a cattle dealer named Dantowitz was reportedly ordered by his fellow stormtroopers to salute, thus offending the dignity of the stormtroopers. The cattle dealer was dragged out and paraded through the city with a wooden sign that read, "This Jewish brat actually dared to ask the stormtroopers to salute him." In Presslau, six Jewish men and six Aryan women were arrested by the police for allegedly having relations. (Havas dispatch, 15th)

(Berlin) Since the incident on Kurfürstendamm last night, anti-Semitic movements have erupted everywhere. Although the police have intervened in many ways, they have been unable to stop them due to the widespread occurrence of incidents. The Polistor Café has been completely destroyed. Hundreds of National Socialists stormed into a cinema because a film about the anti-Semitic movement currently showing was criticized by Jews. They searched the cinema for Jews. Pedestrians and drivers were stopped and inspected by National Socialists to determine whether they were Jews or Aryans. The outbreak of this anti-Semitic movement seems to have been incited by the rhetoric of the National Socialist press. Recently, newspapers have been attacking Jews more fiercely than before. (Havas dispatch, 15th)

(Berlin) This German anti-Semitic movement seems to be a planned affair. The National Socialist Party organ, Der Angriff, published an article a few days ago criticizing [illegible], demanding that National Socialists protest against it. Before the incident on Kurfürstendamm the night before, National Socialists had already held demonstrations in other places. After a period of calm yesterday, disturbances broke out again in the evening. The police fired into the air and patrolled dangerous areas in armored vehicles to prevent incidents. (Havas dispatch, 16th)

(Berlin) The government has recently established a special school to teach air defense knowledge, which is directly under the Air Ministry. The school is responsible for developing and coordinating various air defense methods, as well as training personnel to maintain safety in the event of an enemy air raid. (Havas dispatch, 15th)

160 British Warships Aligned for Ten Miles 64

British Monarch Reviews

(London) Today, the British monarch departed from Portsmouth aboard the royal yacht to review 160 warships offshore. Several hours earlier, a large crowd gathered from Southsea to Portsmouth. Last night was very hot, so thousands of people camped out on the beach to enjoy the spectacle today. The warships were all freshly painted and aligned for ten miles. However, an unfortunate incident occurred. An aircraft carrying passengers from Heathrow Airport to watch the ceremony caught fire and crashed, burning two passengers to death. The pilot and four passengers were unconscious and have been taken to the hospital. (Reuters dispatch, 16th)

(London) King George V, accompanied by the Prince of Wales, the Duke of York, and the Duke of Kent, will travel to Portsmouth Naval Base by special train tomorrow afternoon at approximately 6:00 PM to inspect the naval fleet stationed at home and anchored in the Mediterranean. Upon arrival, the King and his party will proceed to the docks to board the "Victoria" and "Albert" yachts, and then join all cabinet members and naval officers aboard the battleship "Renown," escorted by the battleships "Royal Sovereign" and "Rodney," to conduct the review. The route from the station to the docks in Portsmouth has been decorated with colorful flags and is exceptionally lively. The fleet has positioned its battleships in three rows, with smaller ships at the rear. The fleet stretches for several nautical miles. It is reported that more ships will arrive tomorrow to participate in the review, bringing the total number of warships to 157. In addition, no fewer than several thousand overseas visitors are expected to arrive by nineteen large passenger ships and will be provided with designated landing docks. A fleet of new fishing boats will also participate in the parade, awaiting inspection. (Havas dispatch, 14th)

French Government in All-Day Meetings to Discuss Financial Austerity 65

Will Issue 23 Substitute Laws

(Paris) The French cabinet is preparing to publish new orders and laws tonight to reduce the budget deficit and is therefore holding an unprecedentedly long cabinet meeting. It began at 9:30 AM this morning and lasted until 1:05 PM. The cabinet members then lunched with Prime Minister Laval and reconvened at 2:15 PM. At 6:00 PM, they went to the presidential palace, with President Lebrun presiding, to continue the meeting. (Reuters dispatch, 16th)

(Paris) In order to implement the Financial Powers Act, the Cabinet issued the first substitute law order regarding government austerity on the 3rd of this month, containing three key points: (1) government officials cannot receive multiple salaries for multiple positions; (2) saving administrative expenses of the national defense agencies; (3) establishing a special committee to recommend possible austerity policies. At that time, it was reported that there were still several important measures that would be announced after the National Day on July 14. It is now known that after the State Council meeting adjourns at 6:00 PM tonight, the government will issue 23 substitute law orders, 15 of which relate to saving expenditures to ensure budget balance, and 8 relate to reducing the cost of living and economic recovery. The former 15 substitute law orders are further divided into three categories: (1) stopping waste, (2) reducing extravagance, and (3) substantial government austerity. In addition, there are various special measures to equalize the burden on all levels of the people. Le Matin reported that "the government is striving to reduce expenses on a wide scale, which will save the national treasury 100 million francs." L'Intransigeant reported, "According to Finance Minister Régnier's austerity plan, the salaries of all civil servants, employees, and railway workers, as well as the pensions of war veterans, will be reduced accordingly." However, the wages of miners, unemployment relief funds, and social welfare funds will be paid as usual. The pensions of war veterans will also be re-examined. Widows of soldiers killed in World War I who have remarried will no longer receive the pensions that their deceased husbands were entitled to receive. (Havas dispatch, 16th)

US Treasury Secretary Declares No Change in Silver Policy 66

(Washington) Treasury Secretary Morgenthau reiterated today in response to questions from reporters that there is no change in the U.S. silver policy. Congressional silver proponents also do not acknowledge any further developments. However, experts are very cautious about the future, because although the recent purchase of large quantities of physical silver by the U.S. in London indicates that the U.S. is still active in the silver market, silver prices are still trending downward. (National Telegram, 15th)

(Washington) Senator Thomas, the leader of the Senate silver faction, announced today that his letter to President Roosevelt requesting that the use of silver be expanded and that it be used as the monetary standard along with gold has been signed by 44 senators. Thomas hopes that a majority of senators will sign the letter before it is sent to the White House and said that if the four senators from silver-producing states who have not yet signed and five or six other sympathizers could sign immediately, then the letter could be issued on Tuesday. (National Telegram, 15th)

German Coal Mine Explosion Tragedy 67

Ten Dead, Twenty-Seven Injured

Dortmund, Germany: An explosion occurred today in a coal mine 2,000 feet deep, killing ten people and injuring twenty-seven. It is unknown how many more are buried underground. Because a fire has already started in the mine, rescue efforts are extremely difficult. Many relatives and friends gathered at the mine entrance to watch as rescuers attempted to enter, and many were weeping. (Reuters, 15th)

International Business Telegram — Special Business Report from Reuters on July 16th —

Gold and Silver

British Gold: Today, the price of gold in London rose by two shillings to 140 shillings, eleven and a half pence.

British Silver: The London silver market was quiet today. The spot price was 30 and one-eighth seven five shillings, unchanged. The futures price was 30 and three one two five pence, down 0.0625. Speculators and China sold, while the United States bought. Market conditions are stable.

Exchange Rates

British-American: In the London foreign exchange market this morning, there was a slight demand for gold coins in London, so the price of the pound against the franc fell slightly, and the US exchange rate also fell slightly. The opening exchange rate between the British pound and the US dollar was $4.96375, the same as the closing price of the US-British exchange rate yesterday. It fell half a cent in the first hour, continued to fall 1875 at noon, rose 125 at 1:00 PM, and then fell 0625 at 2:00 PM to $4.9575.

British-French: The opening price rose seven pounds to 74.91 francs, but in the first hour, it fell ten pounds, and at noon it continued to fall two pounds to 74.69 francs, which remained unchanged thereafter.

Cotton and Wheat

American Cotton: The New York cotton market opened higher by several pounds because it was expected that the number of bales remaining at the end of the cotton season would be satisfactory, and because Liverpool prices were stable. However, after the opening, market prices fell, dropping below yesterday's closing price.

British Cotton: The Liverpool cotton market was stable today. At 1:00 PM, the October futures price was 6.25, up three pounds from yesterday's closing price.

British Wheat: The Liverpool wheat market rose slightly this morning due to better American telegrams. At 1:00 PM, the October futures price was four shillings, eleven and seventy-five pence, up eight seven five from yesterday's closing price.

American Wheat: Because Liverpool prices were higher and damage from blight was still being reported, the Chicago wheat market rose at the opening. Then, private news arrived that Canada had a large surplus of wheat available for export, European wheat harvests were not bad, and new American wheat was gradually coming onto the market. Therefore, after the opening, market prices fell back, similar to yesterday's closing prices. Grains are still firm due to spot demand.

Rubber

London: The London rubber market was quiet this morning. At noon, the transaction price for October/December futures was six and sixty-two five pence, unchanged.

New York: New York rubber opened lower because the US consumption figures for June were disappointing. Afterwards, prices gradually loosened, but the quantity of rubber shipped to US ports was less than before, so prices avoided a major drop.

Securities

New York: New York securities opened steadily and mixed. Steel stocks opened slightly higher, but then fell slightly. Railroad stocks continued to be stable. There were no new developments except that the US Court of Appeals declared the Agricultural Adjustment Act unconstitutional. Food stocks were strong as a result of this ruling, while sugar prices loosened. The Dow Jones 30 industrial average opened at ·66, down six pounds. Purchases were as follows:

September New York Silk: 1.355, 1.350, ——, ——, —— (Berlin) After the arrival of the British veterans delegation, they were warmly received by military associations and other groups. Last night, Ribbentrop, Hitler's representative for negotiating disarmament issues, hosted a banquet. Among those invited were key party and state figures, including Minister without Portfolio Hess, representing the Führer Hitler, Minister of Defense General von Blomberg, Interior Minister Dr. Frick, Labor Minister Seldte, Prince August Wilhelm, son of the deposed Kaiser Wilhelm II, and Oberseht, Chairman of the United Association of Victims of the European War. (Havas, 16th)

British Veterans Delegation Received by Key German Figures 68

Former Enemies Shake Hands and Reconcile

(Berlin) The British veterans delegation, invited by the German Nationalist Association, the Disabled Veterans Association, the Steel Helmet League, and the Officers Association, arrived here yesterday. The groups hosted a banquet, during which Ribbentrop, Hitler's representative for negotiating disarmament issues, delivered a speech, stating, "Our goal is to turn veterans of all countries from enemies into friends, especially people from England, France, and Germany. As for the friendship between Germany and England, there is originally nothing to dispute between the two countries. Furthermore, the recent naval agreement between the two countries is a preliminary achievement in establishing peace, which should be clear to the world." Subsequently, Major Gottreley, the chairman of the British delegation, delivered a reply, stating, "Although England only fought against Germany once in the past, from the standpoint of the British veterans delegation, that war was a mistake, and it should not be repeated in the future. Furthermore, I, representing all the veterans of the British Empire, wish to declare to you here that during the Great War, we held the German soldiers in great respect," and so on. After Gottreley finished speaking, he presented the Cross of Honor to the following individuals on behalf of the British Veterans Association: Labor Minister Seldte, Ribbentrop, and Colonel Reinhardt, leader of the German Veterans Association. (Havas, 15th)

(Berlin) This morning, the British veterans delegation laid a wreath at the European War Memorial before visiting Hitler at the Chancellery. Hess also rushed to attend, and disarmament envoy Ribbentrop and Oberlint, president of the Veterans Relief Association, were also present. Oberlint also hosted a banquet for the British delegation at the Kaiserhof Hotel. Ribbentrop spoke the most, first describing the establishment of the Veterans Association, which aims to maintain friendship on the battlefield. The social work achieved by soldiers from England, France, and Germany is admirable. He then stated that he firmly believes that the work accomplished by veterans is valuable, but there is also a historical mission with a broader scope than this work that urgently awaits completion by veterans, and this mission is to harmonize international emotions. Respect for the enemy's spirit fosters friendship between individuals in warring countries, so why can't we develop this spirit from individuals to nations? This is the true mission of veterans. Participating in political movements or influencing the policies of one's own government is not the duty of veterans, but they should create a good situation so that politicians can conclude effective and lasting agreements. England and Germany have no differences. Finally, Ribbentrop quoted Hitler's recent declaration that Germany will do its best to seek friendship with England in order to prevent both countries from experiencing the scourge of war again. Colonel Cortreley, the spokesperson for the British delegation, replied that the delegation believes that the war between the two countries was a major mistake and that it should never happen again. He also believes that lasting peace should be based on mutual respect. At this time of latent crisis, there should be a common bond to ensure security, and that bond is friendship. He and his colleagues firmly believe that this trip will definitely promote Anglo-German friendship. (National News Agency, 15th)

US Senator Opposes US-Russian Trade Agreement, Submits Amendment to Senate 69

(Washington) Senator McCarran opposes the US-Russian trade agreement and opposes Secretary of State Hull's signing of the agreement. Today, he submitted an amendment to the Senate, attaching it to the amendment to the Agricultural Adjustment Act currently under discussion, in order to abolish reciprocal tax rates. McCarran said that the agreement was a "Santa Claus" treaty, calling Hull the "greatest fool in the diplomatic world." What he hates most is that the Soviet Union owes the United States a total of 700 million yuan in debt, of which 400 million yuan is new debt after the Russian Revolution, and has not yet repaid a single penny. Hull has now signed a trade agreement with them. Therefore, he advocates that Congress should immediately withdraw its power to conclude preferential trade agreements. He once said that the US-Russian treaty was not concluded based on reciprocal tax rates, but it is closely related to them, because all the president's privileges come from that bill. Fei also solemnly declared that the agreement only allows Russia to enjoy the same rights as those who have signed trade agreements with other countries, and the condition for the exchange is that Russia promises to purchase goods in the United States. As for the manganese-producing states' claim that after Russian manganese is imported, the American manganese industry will be greatly affected, Fei replied that the entire US manganese industry employs only 354 workers, and the total output is only 10% of US usage. (National News Agency, 15th)

Japan Plans to Build Tunnel Under Kanmon Straits 71

(Tokyo) Technician Kato, dispatched by the Ministry of Home Affairs to survey the site of the Kanmon Straits National Highway Tunnel, has completed preliminary investigations and consulted with the military. The specific plan decided by the Ministry of Home Affairs is to build a tunnel under the Hayatomo Strait at a total cost of 8 million yen. Geological surveys will take two years, and the tunnel construction will take three years. The plan is as follows: (1) On the Shimonoseki side, a 1,400-meter tunnel will be built under the Maeda area of Danoura. From the center of the tunnel, a tunnel will be excavated to connect to the seabed, exiting at Moji Nagasaki, and then passing through a 720-meter tunnel to the surface. (2) The tunnel will be 7.5 meters wide, separating roads for cars and bicycles. (3) At the intersection of the underground tunnel of the national highway on the Shimonoseki side and the undersea tunnel, a Rotunda-style traffic control device will be installed. (Dentsu, 16th)

River Water Has Receded Slightly, Wuhan Embankments Still in Danger, Zhang Embankment Has Hundreds of Holes and is Full of Peril, Exploding Pinghan Railway Tracks to Divert Xiang River into Yangtze River 72

Hankou Communication: The river water receded by two inches today. Although the Wuhan dikes are no less dangerous, this has greatly comforted the citizens. A section of the Wuchang Hui Embankment Yongbao Sluice was found to have collapsed inward today. On the Wuwei Road side of the Wutai Sluice, the embankment collapsed by a length of more than ten feet. The Wujin Embankment also collapsed by three feet. Troops sent by the garrison headquarters, together with rescue workers, desperately tried to rescue it and have plugged all the gaps. Among them, the Wu Hui Embankment is riddled with holes and has become incurable. It is still feared that it will inevitably collapse. The rice fields inside the embankment will be ripe soon, and can be harvested in three or four days if they can last. Therefore, although it is known that defense is impossible, one has to do one's best. It has been discovered that the Zhang Gong Embankment in Hankou has ten sections of collapse, including Huangjiawan, Jinkou, Gusaoshu, Jinyin Lake, Fenjin Furnace, Zhayan Port, Chen Yangjing, Huangjiashangwan, Xiawan, Xiaowan, and others. The section at Gusaoshu is the most dangerous. On the 14th, that section collapsed very long. After 20,000 people tried to rescue it, it was repaired this morning. Another section in the same place was found to have collapsed again today, about thirty feet long. The "Bao" character watchtower at the corner of the embankment is leaking about a hundred meters, and the "He" character watchtower is also leaking, with the risk of the entire embankment collapsing. Ye Peng, who is in charge of flood control, was ordered to command the municipal government, the Jianghan Engineering Bureau, and military and police and civilians to station at the embankment for rescue. An office was established on the 14th, and general mobilization continued today. The most dangerous section of Gusaoshu is commanded by Ye himself, the Daijiashan embankment corner is commanded by Mayor Wu Guozhen, and the Jinkou section is commanded by Jin Jutang, chief of staff of the military police department, with complete wartime preparations. A temporary military court was also organized at Gusaoshu to enforce rescue efforts under military law. The office was established on the 15th and immediately issued a notice saying, "For the purpose of notifying everyone, the Zhang Gong Embankment is of great importance to the safety of life and property of more than 800,000 people in Hankou. This commander will supervise the rescue efforts to reverse the crisis. All employees should be disciplined according to military law. Those who disobey orders, or do not abide by discipline, or do not take responsibility, or neglect their duties, will be severely punished according to military law depending on the severity of the circumstances. Those who work hard and establish achievements will also be rewarded according to their merits. It is hereby announced so that everyone is aware." Ye said that the Zhang Gong Embankment is diseased all over, and is full of perils. Having been appointed in a time of danger, I will be driven by my conscience, and I am determined to take responsibility and do my best. I am currently working on organizing the embankment defense workers, with soldiers from the garrison brigade as squad leaders, squad leaders as platoon leaders, and platoon leaders as company commanders, all militarized to ensure discipline and communication. If an accident unfortunately occurs, it will be dealt with according to military law. Ye also said that the water level of the Xiang River is too high, and the embankment is too thin to withstand the pressure of the flood, resulting in extreme danger. He specifically reported to Zhang Xueliang, the director of the garrison headquarters. At 5:00 PM on the 15th, Zhang sent a battalion of engineers to the embankment corner to destroy the Pinghan Railway tracks at Chenjiaji, in order to release the Xiang River water outside the embankment into the Yangtze River, which was also quite effective. If the river does not rise again, lives can be saved. It is noted that after the disaster in 1931, the Jianghan Engineering Bureau was responsible for the repair and defense of the embankment, but the section below Danshui Pool was contracted by the Hankou Municipal Government. The dangers this time occurred within the scope contracted by the Jianghan Engineering Bureau. Yang Silian, the director of the bureau, has rarely been at work during the days of rescue, which has aroused the dissatisfaction of the citizens. He suddenly resigned on the 14th, which is no different from desertion. Although he claimed to be recuperating, there is no trace of him. All newspapers have reported this in detail on the 15th. Also, the flood control funds for this year were approved by the Economic Commission for 200,000 yuan, and later increased by 100,000 yuan, totaling 300,000 yuan. As of the 14th, Yang had spent 370,000 yuan. All subsequent expenses have not been settled. Zhang Qun, the chairman of the provincial government, has urgently telegraphed Chairman Chiang to ask the Economic Commission to allocate an additional 200,000 yuan for flood control to relieve the emergency and avoid delays. When the dikes were alarming, Gao Yihan, the inspector of the two lakes, repeatedly sent personnel to the dikes for inspection, strictly examining the diligence and laziness of the staff, and secretly investigating whether the repair personnel had dereliction of duty. If there are those who fail to repair the dikes effectively, they will be impeached according to the facts. (15th)

Shashi Submerged in Water, General Embankment Still Safe, Corpses of People and Animals Drifting Downstream, Food Shortage, Homes Gone 73

The Zi Lin Bao Shashi correspondent reported that Shashi City is now under water, and the city is full of hungry people whose fate depends entirely on the support of the general embankment around the city. The embankment still stands today, but after the great flood, there are many gaps. It is now fixed with the last bean bags. After the water has caused the beans to swell, the gaps can be filled. Shashi was flooded in several places on July 3rd when the river water rose sharply. On the 5th and 6th, there was heavy rain, so the river water was even higher. Jingzhou City, which is located lower, is surrounded by water. The city gates were quickly closed to prevent the influx of huge torrents. Foreigners in Shashi hired a boat and sent several brave people to rescue the county magistrate, but because the heavy rain continued and the water level gradually rose, it was difficult to do anything. Thousands of foreigners and refugees gathered on the large pile of stacks on the slope of the general embankment, where the Shashi packaging factory is also located. Before long, the Shashi Needle Felt China Bank branch, the Bank of Communications branch, etc., sent their valuable documents and deposits to that place. But the victims kept coming, and there was almost no room to accommodate them. The place is about fifteen to twenty feet below the water surface. Before long, the water suddenly dropped by a foot, which must have been caused by a breach in the embankment. It was then learned that there was a breach upstream and downstream, and the low-lying areas had become a swamp. It was also heard that the county magistrate and the people trapped in Jingzhou City were suffering the calamity of fish. On the 7th, more and more refugees came, because their homes had all been submerged. Fortunately, the general embankment is still safe today, but there is a shortage of food and homes have disappeared. Trees and complete houses are often seen floating in the water, with all the doors and windows intact. It is feared that there are still people living inside. The corpses of people and animals and various utensils are drifting downstream, too many to count, and it is shocking to see. The heavy rain stopped on the 7th, but the flood had no sign of receding on the following day. On the 9th, Western women and other powerful people in the city took refuge downstream on Wuhu steamers passing through Yichang. Foreign men remained here. The water gradually receded on that day.

Shandong Yellow River Breach Water Passes Through Jining, Main River Water Has Fallen Significantly, Middle and Lower Reaches Still in Emergency 74

Jinan Communication: Regarding the situation of the breach of the Yellow River in Yu Xi, according to the long-distance telephone report from Jining last night (14th), the Yellow River water is still continuing to flow southeast. One branch flowing towards Yuncheng County has completely passed through the county, entering the Zhu River and the Zhao Wang River in the southeast, flowing southeast along the riverbed, and heading towards Nanyang Lake. On the afternoon of the 14th, the flood water had already passed Jining to the south (25 miles west of Jining City). Jining County Magistrate Zhen Guangyuan convened an emergency meeting. Fearing that the flood water would continue to flow southeast and overflow eastward, the county urgently mobilized civilians, day and night, to build civil levees on the east side of the river, raising and thickening them to prevent the Yellow River water from flooding eastward. The water flowing towards Juye has reached the Lijiazhuang and Huangzhuang areas in Jiaxiang County, not far from the city. Jiaxiang is rushing to build civil levees to protect the city and prevent flooding. This water flow is extremely vast, with no end in sight, and the water head is more than two meters high. The water flowing towards Heze has reached the Qili River area. County Magistrate Chen Yizhi supervised and led civilians to build dikes along the river to defend. The water flowing towards Dongping has reached Daimiao, 25 miles west of the city. The water flow is so large that it has breached two openings on the south bank of the Qing River, flowing towards Nanwang Lake and Shushan Lake. As for the Yellow River water level, it is continuing to fall. At 6:00 PM on the 14th, the River Affairs Bureau reported that Damajia in the lower reaches fell by 3 centimeters, the water level was 14 meters and 8 centimeters. Xieziwan fell by 6 inches and 6 points, the water level was 18 meters, 7 inches and 7 points. Guanzhuang in the middle reaches fell by 5 inches and 1 point, the water level was 34 meters, 2 inches and 7 points. Luokou fell by 9 centimeters, the water level was 29 meters, and there was no danger.

In Shandong Province, in addition to the first breach which is still easy to block, the other breaches in the upper reaches of the Yellow River have large and rapid water flows, and are likely to merge into one. Zhang Lianjia, the director of the River Affairs Bureau, and Han Duofeng, the inspector sent by the provincial government, both believe that the river water is too large and construction is difficult, and have requested that materials be prepared and the blocking be carried out after the water flow has subsided slightly. However, Li Yishe, the chairman of the Benefit Committee, sent a telegram urging the River Affairs Bureau to dredge and block the breach. Li also inspected the Dongzhuang breach with Kong Xiangrong. Seeing the serious situation, they requested that post-disaster relief be arranged quickly. Zhang Xuanxiao, Jia Han Duofeng and Sun Zherang are now discussing solutions in Dongzhuang. The water from the breach has entered the Zhu River and is spreading eastward. All counties are rushing to repair dikes. From Qili River to Jining Nanyang Lake, the river defenses are flooded. In the Heze branch, there is a tendency to change course and follow the old course of the Yellow River. The middle and lower reaches are still in urgent need of assistance. According to the disaster report inspected by Han Duofeng, the situation is extremely tragic. Han Fuju intends to send a telegram to expand the scope of begging for assistance in order to save the victims. (15th)

Minister Chiang Kai-shek's Speech on the Responsibilities of Youth (Continued) - Chengdu Attendance at Expanded Memorial Week 75

The points mentioned above are to explain the responsibilities and cultivation that you young people should shoulder. I believe you all understand them very well. Now, I can use two sentences that I often say to summarize the principles mentioned earlier, which are: "The purpose of life is to enhance the life of all mankind; the meaning of life is to create the continuous life of the universe." This is where the meaning and purpose of our existence lie. Many of the things mentioned above can be summarized into these two sentences. Everyone should know that heaven, earth, parents gave birth to us, and society and the nation educated us, making us grow up, read, and learn skills. What is the value and purpose of all this? If it is for personal glory and wealth, for clothes to wear and food to eat, then one is an unambitious and unpromising person. This is not the purpose for which parents gave birth to me, society and the nation raised me, and schools educated me. The fundamental purpose of our birth, growth, education, and learning is to save the nation, save our compatriots, and especially to seek happiness for the majority of poor compatriots, to enhance the lives of all mankind. Moreover, life is only a few decades long and will eventually end in death. We must be able to inherit the historical life of our ancestors and parents and create new life for future generations, so that the new life of the universe will flow and progress endlessly. Only then, although our bodies may die, our spiritual life can be in harmony with the universe. Only in this way will our life have true meaning. We are human beings, and each individual should live a purposeful and meaningful life. Therefore, we must strive and sacrifice everything to enhance the lives of people and create the life of the universe. For example, now we must work hard to carry out the suppression of bandits and the revolutionary cause of national revival, and this is how it is. Secondly, to fulfill our extraordinary responsibility of saving the nation and the people, we must have many important conditions, of course, but the most important condition is to first have a strong physique. With a strong physique, we can then have a strong spirit, be able to shoulder heavy responsibilities and go far, endure hardship and hard work, and accomplish great undertakings. This is a very obvious principle, and everyone must know it. I think that the physique of you young students is really too poor. Like today, you have been standing here for less than an hour, and it is still morning, not the most intense time of the sun, but many people have fainted today. With such a poor physique, how can you save the nation? You must know that now, young students are fighting with sunlight, air, and cold water all day long, regardless of how hot or cold it is, how strong the wind is, how deep the water is, or how heavy the rain and snow are. They are always practicing running, carrying heavy loads and climbing mountains, or swimming. These things, and the hotter the weather and the heavier the rain and snow, the more energetic they are and the more vigorously they practice. Therefore, young people are able to have strong physiques and vigorous spirits, and the entire country and nation are also very strong as a result. Therefore, if we want to do great things in the future and save the nation, we must also intensify physical training. School principals, faculty, and parents must pay attention to students' physical education and no longer listen to them hiding in houses to avoid sunlight, rain, cold, and heat, developing into weak and listless sick men, as in the past. Moreover, to improve physical education, it is not enough to rely solely on one or two hours of exercise or sports on the playground every day. We must also pay attention to organizing the following various training activities: First, extracurricular competitions. All kinds of competitions that are beneficial to the body should be held once a week for small competitions and once a month for large competitions to increase students' interest in physical education and cultivate their habit of exercise. Second, field exercises, such as hiking trips of dozens or more than ten miles, swimming, mountain climbing, running, and other exercises, are all very beneficial to physical education and should be held frequently. Third, camping exercises. Although the general Boy Scouts are said to have camping exercises, they are too few. In the future, not only the Boy Scouts but also the students of each school should hold them once a month to cultivate their habit of competing with nature, thereby strengthening their physique, boosting their spirits, and enhancing their courage. Fourth, labor service, that is, as mentioned earlier, the daily life affairs of the family and school, whatever they can do and should do, they should do themselves to cultivate the habit of labor. They should also serve their parents, teachers, friends, and the general public in society to promote the spirit of service. In this way, they can also get opportunities for exercise. In any case, school faculty and family elders should always think of various ways to train the physique of their students and children, making them a citizen who can compete with any difficulties and dangers. At the same time, they should also pay attention to medicine and hygiene, prevent diseases, and immediately treat students if they become ill. Physical examinations should also be conducted once a month to see how their physical strength changes. Those who have increased their physical strength should be given special rewards to encourage everyone to pay attention to cultivation and physical training. Those whose bodies have become weaker should also be given special warnings and exhortations to pay attention to training and turn weakness into strength. This is a very important matter, and school principals and faculty should pay special attention to it. In addition, there is another matter concerning educational policy that school principals and faculty should also pay attention to, which is to promote production education. The most important part of production education is agricultural production education. Each school should specially set aside a piece of land as a place for students to engage in supplementary farming, gardening, and animal husbandry, so as to arouse students' habit of labor and interest in agricultural production, as well as knowledge and skills. In the future, when they graduate and return to their hometowns, they can engage in agriculture and animal husbandry, becoming independent producers of society and the nation, and not parasites dependent on families and society. At present, schools have not paid attention to this point, which is really a major shortcoming of education. I hope those responsible for education will think of ways to achieve this, and students should also understand this principle and learn this essential skill for earning a living that Chinese citizens must have.

Finally, I have one more suggestion to offer to the principals and faculty of all universities and middle schools, that is, you should refer to the current laws and regulations to organize a faculty group, a group for joint research and discussion of this kind. The purpose of organizing this group is to enable all of you faculty members to keep pace with the times in terms of first-rate knowledge, physique, and spirit, and to set an example for students, leading them to become healthy citizens. You should also hold meetings frequently to discuss and improve education and all practical and feasible methods. Even things that our faculty members cannot do themselves can be submitted to the educational administrative authorities for adoption. Furthermore, we must jointly and consistently maintain the school's discipline and the overall academic atmosphere, so that education can improve every day. I have many ideas about this method, but I cannot elaborate on them today. Please study and consider them yourselves. In any case, I hope that all principals and faculty members will make special efforts to ensure that Chengdu's education can change with each passing day and become a model for education in the whole country. I hope that all of you will adhere to this grand purpose and move forward to fulfill the responsibility of saving the nation through education, so as not to fail the deep expectations of the nation and the people. Since I came to Chengdu, I have spoken to leaders from all walks of life six times, and each time I have talked about the direction and essence of education. If you can all do it conscientiously, I believe that with the progress of education, it will not only be easy to build a new Sichuan, but also to quickly build a brand-new Republic of China. Today, because the weather is very hot and you Boy Scouts have not developed the ability to compete with the sun on a regular basis, many people have been unable to hold on. Therefore, today I have only talked about a few programs in general. The principles in them should be elaborated on in detail by you group leaders, principals, and faculty members to tell your students, especially to pay attention to physical training, so that at least when you convene and speak again, no one will faint again, so that everyone can become upright young students, self-reliant, and healthy citizens with independent personalities, able to build on the past and open up the future, save our country, and revive our Chinese nation, worthy of being descendants of the Yellow Emperor and citizens of the Republic of China. (July 10)

Chen Fugen, a key suspect in the kidnapping and murder of Han Jingsheng, a wealthy businessman from Wuxi, is 28 years old and from Wuxi. Wuxi - Tea and Restaurant Industry Requests Removal of Harsh Taxes 78

The Wuxi Tea and Restaurant Industry Association believes that the tea tax and banquet tax in Wuxi are harsh and should be abolished. They have repeatedly telegraphed the Jiangsu Provincial Donation and Tax Supervision Committee, requesting their abolition. The Tax Supervision Committee raised the issue for discussion at a meeting and resolved: (1) Although the tea tax is considered to be abolished, according to the investigation by Commissioner Zhang Zhongren, local people in the county have requested that it be temporarily retained and should be decided at the final summary meeting after the entire investigation is completed. (2) The banquet tax is a luxury consumption and is not among those to be abolished. Moreover, the regulations are common in all counties, and the tax rate is only 5 percent, with exemptions for amounts below 2 yuan, which does not harm integrity and should not be discussed. The Supervision Committee has copied the draft resolution and sent it to the Wuxi Chamber of Commerce for separate notification.

Changzhou - Red Swastika Society Establishes Large-Scale Hospital 79

The Changzhou Red Swastika Society, considering that the city and suburbs have a population of 150,000 and the entire county has nearly a million, but there are very few hospitals available for patients to recuperate, raised funds to establish the Red Swastika Society Hospital in Maxiang. It temporarily has 50 beds, divided into first, second, and third class and maternity wards. It has everything, including light · purple light · sun lamps · electrotherapy equipment · surgical laboratories, etc. Chen Shunming has been hired as the director, and Cheng Yangxian, Cai Jun, and Zhao Pinlian as physicians, specializing in internal medicine, surgery, dermatology, pediatrics, obstetrics, and ophthalmology, otolaryngology. Preparations have been underway for half a year, and they are now nearing completion. The hospital is scheduled to open on the 20th of this month. Since it is the height of summer, with epidemics rampant, outpatient consultations will be free for one month, specializing in serving the poor and sick.

Changshu - Donglai Town Attacked by Bandits Again 80

At the intersection of the fourth and seventh districts of this county, there is a newly emerging market town called Donglai Town, which is quite prosperous in commerce. The entire town was suddenly robbed by bandits the year before last. Unexpectedly, on the morning of the 15th, it was attacked by bandits again. The home of Fang Yulan, a villager of the first household of the first Jia of the sixth Bao in the town, was suddenly attacked by several bandits, all armed with guns and white cloths wrapped around their heads. After entering, they tied up all the members of the family, young and old, and poured cold water all over Fang Yulan. Fortunately, the ropes binding him were slightly loose, and he was able to escape through the back door to Sishui, where he reported to the town's commercial corps. The corps then went to surround Fang's residence. When the bandits heard the alarm, they fired guns to resist arrest. The commercial corps also returned fire, and after about a few minutes, the bandits were defeated and all escaped through the back door to Sishui, with none captured. Later, they heard the victim calling for help and realized that the bandits had gone far away. According to statistics, the losses amounted to about 1,000 taels of silver. They also picked up 14 items left behind by the bandits, including the National Evening News and the Xibao, one each. It is suspected that the bandits came from the Xijing area.

Joint Establishment of Epidemic Prevention Zone by the Ministry and Province 83

The Ministry of Industry and Commerce considers Dongyang County in Zhejiang Province to be a famous area for producing ham, but in recent years, animal epidemics have been prevalent, causing a large number of deaths and greatly affecting the rural economy. Rescuing Industry and Commerce - National Treasury Vouchers Issued Yesterday - The Loan Review Committee Urges the Ministry of Finance to Approve Measures 84

The Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Loan Review Committee received national treasury vouchers worth 20 million yuan yesterday afternoon as the second guarantee for rescuing industrial and commercial loans, and will send them to the China National Products Bank for safekeeping. The Committee is using 15 million yuan of these national treasury vouchers as the second guarantee for mortgage loans. As the regulations for banks and money shops to undertake these loans have not yet been instructed by the Ministry of Finance, it was resolved at the fifth meeting to request instructions from the Ministry, and a letter urging the Ministry was also recorded and sent yesterday. The details are as follows:

National Treasury Vouchers Issued Yesterday

The Ministry of Finance allocated national treasury vouchers worth 20 million yuan as the second guarantee for industrial and commercial mortgage loans. The Loan Review Committee previously established measures for the custody and use of the vouchers with the China National Products Bank. After being approved by the Ministry, the vouchers were issued to the Committee at 3:00 PM yesterday. The vouchers consist of twenty pieces, each worth one million yuan. The Committee is scheduled to send them to the China National Products Bank for safekeeping today and tomorrow.

Urging the Ministry of Finance to Approve Measures

In recent days, the industrial and commercial sectors have been quite concerned about loan matters and have been going to the Loan Review Committee to inquire about the exact measures for mortgage loans. The Committee believes that the Ministry of Finance has not yet approved the measures for banks and money shops to undertake these loans. Therefore, this point was raised for discussion at the fifth meeting a few days ago, and it was resolved to request instructions from the Ministry on whether this mortgage loan has been decided, and which bank or money shop will undertake it. If it has not been decided, then the Ministry is requested to promptly order the banks and money shops to negotiate and agree on the undertaking as soon as possible. If the Ministry has other measures, it is also requested to approve them as soon as possible. The Committee Chairman, Mr. Cai Zengji, has already recorded a letter to the Ministry requesting instructions yesterday.

National Products Manufacturers Request Urgent Rescue

The National Products Manufacturers Association believes that credit mortgage loans are far from certain. Yesterday, they sent a special letter to Cai Zengji, Chairman of the Industrial and Commercial Loan Review Committee, stating: "Dear Sir, in recent years, disasters have been frequent, and the people's livelihood is haggard. Coupled with the impact of the global economic recession and the devastation of the American silver policy, the countryside is gradually going bankrupt, and cities are collapsing one after another. Shanghai is the national industrial and commercial center, and the impact is such that the market is deteriorating. Since the year-end accounts of the previous year, the financial turmoil has been dangerous, and factories and shops have closed down one after another. The crisis of the economic situation and the shock to social order are unprecedented. For self-preservation, the industrial and commercial community has appealed to the authorities to coordinate rescue efforts. The government has taken pity on the people's plight and attached importance to the national foundation, and has issued 100 million yuan in financial public bonds to consolidate the credit of banks, 15 million yuan in mortgage loans, and 5 million yuan in credit loans to save industry and commerce, and has gathered talented people to organize a Loan Review Committee to jointly save the crisis, and has appointed you, sir, as the Chairman. You, sir, are an advanced member of the Party and the country, and have been in charge of Shanghai's finances for many years. You are familiar with the situation and are deeply gratified to have found the right person. However, industry and commerce are in a critical situation and urgently need the government's loans to be realized as soon as possible. They are eagerly looking forward to prolonging their survival. For four months, news has spread in the newspapers that plans have been made to rescue industry and commerce, and that loans for rescue are about to be realized. However, the actual framework for the loans only began to be finalized on the 9th with the approval of the Ministry of Finance. The procedures and measures for credit loans and mortgage loans are extremely slow and tortuous. The 15 million yuan mortgage loan must be made by each bank itself, reported to the Loan Review Committee for review, and then the national treasury vouchers will be issued as the second guarantee. The banks and money shops that have been identified for credit loans have not yet registered. The mortgage loans must also be submitted by your Committee to the Ministry of Finance for inquiry, and it is unclear whether the participating banks and money shops have been decided. In this situation, the date of realization of credit loans and mortgage loans is unknown. Even if they are realized, Shanghai's industry and commerce will inevitably collapse due to unbearable fatigue. Moreover, the funds for rescue are entrusted to banks and money shops that are difficult to protect themselves, and the review of loans is controlled by your Committee. The request for rescue from banks and money shops should come before the request for rescue from industry and commerce. The fire is already raging, but the brave warriors who claim to be firefighters are still drowsy. What in the world is more unpredictable than this? You, sir, are familiar with the situation and know the situation well. We earnestly implore you to understand our suffering and speak frankly to the authorities, to rescue industry and commerce from danger, and to save the people's livelihood from overturning. A single word can revitalize a country, and we hope you, sir, will plan for it."

Sailing Ship Passengers Carrying Silver Coins - Customs Regulations Limit the Amount - Each Ship is Only Allowed to Carry 100 Yuan in Silver Coins 85

Tang Haian, Superintendent of the Jianghai Customs, and Loford, Commissioner of Customs, issued Joint Announcement No. 2530 yesterday regarding the Ministry's order to regulate the limited amount of silver coins carried by sailing ship crew members and passengers, stating: "The measures for suppressing the smuggling of silver coins or silver out of the country have been announced repeatedly. Now, according to the order of the Ministry of Finance, it is stipulated that all sailing ships operating on the sea surface from Yantai, Qingdao, Longkou, and other coastal ports, regardless of crew members or passengers, are only allowed to carry a total of 100 yuan in silver coins per ship. Those exceeding the limit must hold a passport issued by the Ministry before being allowed to pass. Those without a passport will be confiscated to show the limit. All ship merchants must be informed of this announcement."

Closure of the Banque Franco-Chinoise Branch in Xiamen - Debtors Wire Shanghai for Help 91

According to the Central News Agency, the Banque Franco-Chinoise has absorbed a considerable amount of Chinese currency since its establishment. Depositors are now aware that the bank's absorption of large sums of money has a significant impact on the national and social economy, so they have been withdrawing their deposits one after another. Branches in various locations have also been closing down one after another, resulting in significant losses for depositors. After the Xiamen branch suddenly closed on July 1st, all responsible personnel fled. The thousands of depositors in the area formed the Xiamen Banque Franco-Chinoise Creditors' Group to jointly address the situation. The group sent an express mail telegram to appeal to all sectors of society across the country. The original telegram stated: "The Banque Franco-Chinoise has established branches throughout the country, absorbing a significant amount of currency. Considering just the Xiamen branch and the Zhangzhou, Quanzhou, Anhai, and Kinmen sub-branches, the amount is in the millions. People in society, due to its prize-linked savings, which resembles gambling, have been opposing and denouncing it. On July 1st of this year, the Xiamen branch suddenly closed down. Manager He Chengzhi and key personnel Liang Jiliu and Liang Youquan had already fled without a trace. The Zhangzhou and Quanzhou sub-branches also closed down simultaneously. Like a bolt from the blue, the masses were shocked. Depositors gathered on July 4th to form a creditors' group and petitioned the Xiamen Municipal Public Security Bureau and the local court to arrest and investigate. It has been found that the branch committed fraud on a large scale and intentionally absconded. Most of the depositors are ordinary people, and their hard-earned savings have been lost, causing deep pain and suffering. The financial turmoil is affecting the social economy, causing even greater harm. We urgently request the leaders of the Party and the country to uphold justice and impose strict sanctions. We also hope that depositors in various locations will unite and form creditors' groups to jointly address the situation, thereby promoting liquidation and protecting their rights and interests. The national economy and the people's livelihood depend on this. We hereby report this by telegram. Respectfully, representatives of the Xiamen Banque Franco-Chinoise Creditors' Group, Wu Kebin, Yang Xing, Sun Deqi, and others, along with thousands of depositors, respectfully appeal."

Shanghai County Reclassified as Third Class 92

Shanghai County's administrative expenses were originally classified as first class. Now, according to a provincial order, it has been reclassified as third class, effective from this year. Therefore, the county government will reallocate the funds starting this month to comply with the provincial regulations.

County-Owned Properties Must Be Paid for Within a Deadline 93

The Shanghai County Government received an order yesterday from the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance stating that if any people have occupied local government properties without paying for them, they must report it voluntarily within three months and pay according to regulations. If they fail to report within the deadline, the properties will be put up for public auction. The original occupants will not be allowed to make excuses to claim ownership. If anyone relies on force to occupy the properties, once discovered or reported by others, in addition to returning the land price according to regulations, they will also be subject to a fine. If it is reported by others, half of the fine will be given as a reward. The public should be informed and ordered to report within the deadline.
